# 全国主要城市出租车｜何以为龢

来源：https://www.yuque.com/chaofun/tuxun/cn_taxi_major_city

全国主要城市（市区）出租车

ps:此文档仅介绍地图街景拍摄时的出租车，不是城市最新营运的出租车！

可能会有型号配色不全等问题，请联系

何以为龢

。图片均来源于百度&Google地图。

       在中国匹配中，出租车是区域定位的重要线索，也是一个城市的特色和象征，您可以根据其配色和车型确定您所在的城市，是快速定位得分的关键。以下是全国主要城市（市区）出租车的详细介绍:

## 第一部分  直辖市

#### 1.北京市

- 主要为现代伊兰特（图二图四）、悦动（图一图五）、北汽绅宝D50（图六）和北京EU5（图三图七）四种车型

北京市出租车的配色种类虽多，但是车型较有特点且富有城市特色，较好辨认。

​

#### 2.天津市

- 车型种类较多，主要为丰田花冠（图一），大众捷达（图二）和一汽威志 V5（图三图四），其他车型能见度较低（如图五图六）

![9e599ee6a88e1fc2b4082ca20913a5f.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754130147519-a0840892-0c4d-46a1-b813-2d38af27cccc.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_17%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![c82dfb1d008e12de52388fa8d1bf367.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754130162720-11f3814b-a135-452f-9016-a2d2cc6e8370.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/jpeg/35193536/1707735930267-8c08ba58-263e-4437-a327-add62fefe8fd.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![feedcf65fa06d05b26ef2760d7980a6.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754130181216-99f76ab5-9ead-4a27-8cf0-309256b707c4.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![05331c381c93c5c6defe506c0e3bf18.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754130261528-645c0107-f3dc-4186-a574-dcdc68cef250.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_15%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![44103ebe42c8157cba8c4db70a2542c.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754130270220-ad2b8491-abed-4288-a482-1254edb4a8f1.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

天津市出租车有着统一的青银配色，特点是顶灯有黄白两种且结构简单。

​

#### 3.上海市

- 品牌以大众、荣威为主

![e79d2182268152ed7a28b2d24edacce.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754131389286-dadfba93-127a-483c-862c-2dcfd8689af0.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![9934410375fe6f0a2f5a364128294a8.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754131410355-bdcaedda-a0cf-430a-a838-0af059e46721.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![abdcf9f027fbae2af916fc5ae26eb92.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754131420038-7af712ee-a3d2-4e8c-b1f1-931cff35e498.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![6a7857b345b7e0cb8300a41107abfd5.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754131427211-cfe9dcb3-864b-46b7-873c-2569da61ae88.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_18%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![2e29a8317554316c3cccd48a9d20178.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754131441350-b1669c60-c6cf-4a71-b1bb-4b3bd5174441.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_18%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

以上是其部分车型及配色

由于上海市街景更新较为频繁，覆盖跨度比较长，导致街景中出租车的型号配色杂乱不一。虽然不易记忆，但好在其城市特征明显，也算较好辨认。如遇请寻找题目中更多信息来进一步佐证您的猜想。

​

#### 4.重庆市

重庆市出租车的型号配色较为统一，整车为黄色涂装且顶灯竖放，极好辨认。如遇请大胆选择重庆市。

更加详细的重庆出租车介绍请移步「[重庆市｜人生河海](https://www.yuque.com/chaofun/tuxun/chongqing#td1Rk)」

## 第二部分  各省（自治区）主要城市

#### 黑龙江省

##### 1.哈尔滨市

- 主要为大众捷达/桑塔纳（除图二、六、十），黑色礼宾车为丰田凯美瑞（图十）和福特蒙迪欧两款车型（ ★ 配色重点记忆）

![0773c1be6c94ea100dc43091d6bd76e7.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1762681181187-f9b7de19-ae6d-4622-b975-56489a92cbfb.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_29%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![aed091ae1741ed20f0b375b86600e83f.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1762681772198-eb6103d2-0f7c-4c5f-9bc6-4c16915b0d09.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

哈尔滨市出租车配色种类较多，其中蓝顶橙车身数量最多，但早期上蓝下银配色能见度最高。特点是车牌上方的白色小牌子。车侧的艺术体TAXI在黑龙江许多城市出租车上都有出现。

##### 2.齐齐哈尔市

- 大多为大众捷达/桑塔纳（图一至三，图七）

齐齐哈尔市出租车型号及配色种类较多，车前方一般都配有圆弧小牌子，部分车侧的贴纸上有“齐市”字样，且引擎盖上印有圆滑体的"TAXI"。

##### 3.牡丹江市

- 车型种类较多，品牌主要为铃木（图一图四），起亚（图二图三）

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738248825382-7cb88475-8c8e-4d99-92b6-452450403f5a.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_27%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

牡丹江市出租车基本上为蓝银和红底黑白条配色，有少量绿银及其他配色。

##### 4.佳木斯市

- 主要为大众捷达/桑塔纳（图一图二）和现代伊兰特（图三图五）

佳木斯市出租车配色较为统一，前车牌上方均配有黄色方形牌子，且车顶也印有白色四位编码，较好辨认。

大庆市出租车共有六种配色，但下底均为银色。车侧椭圆形 TAXI 贴纸较有特色，易于辨认。

#### 吉林省

长春市出租车配色种类丰富，其中银橙和白橙两种（区别不大）能见度最高。多在车侧后门上印着服务监督电话。

- 基本上为大众捷达/桑塔纳（除图六）

吉林市出租车配色种类虽多但较有特色，其中白绿配色最为常见。一般车头左边及车尾右边都配有蓝色圆弧小牌子，较好辨认。

##### 3.四平市

- 蓝银配色中一汽威志（图一）和大众捷达（图二）居多，白绿配色以铃木羚羊（图四）和夏利N3（图五）为主

四平市出租车型号配色较为统一，车头左边和车尾右边的白色小牌子是其特点，易于辨认。

##### 4.辽源市

- 基本上为大众捷达（除图三）

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=245696684140221466&skey=@crypt_c5903577_4cfd908b196661c18808151dbab401c8&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769924944873-dd95ccd5-3456-4777-be09-dd37ae093185.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=5714437578763110808&skey=@crypt_c5903577_4cfd908b196661c18808151dbab401c8&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769924998672-26a9ae79-0ed1-49af-8aba-de8c22eb5317.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=7584389152048531524&skey=@crypt_c5903577_4cfd908b196661c18808151dbab401c8&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769925031359-059b308a-9220-4dd7-bbe6-0181057e055a.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=196784929256511275&skey=@crypt_c5903577_4cfd908b196661c18808151dbab401c8&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769925061357-be851024-e409-4cb6-8b57-8beef85e2200.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=6688642777834207280&skey=@crypt_c5903577_4cfd908b196661c18808151dbab401c8&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769925069046-539549b8-50e0-4141-afba-e58fd705bd0f.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

辽源市出租车型号统一，配色为五种不同涂装样式的白绿，且车侧印字多为红色。

##### 5.白城市

- 基本上为大众捷达

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738237754531-80481465-0a42-4645-a7c8-12a7aecb4b99.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_27%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738237933607-66b07046-e827-43cb-8f65-6999f13049fc.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738238038882-b664371c-43dd-40fa-ab98-10f0413f55f9.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_30%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

白城市出租车配色统一为白底绿色线条。白城别称“鹤城”，因此车侧有印着鹤状标志；除此之外，车左前方的红色牌子也是其特点。

​

#### 辽宁省

##### 1.沈阳市

- 车型种类较多，但多为现代悦动（图一）和铃木启悦（图三）。早期以大众捷达为主

![3d161535731b955eadf33d6aca969535.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1762683528439-b2693304-619e-41ee-bc27-8b8a528a21e1.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![f590538cb871a650ee3dbf8e25d99ff5.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1762683553656-f265417e-1fed-4561-adf1-b18dff79447e.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_31%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![e0a819df92db80700e91cd6585f80b67.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1762684202677-6bf1ae77-85cc-4da6-b5c7-1f97fb730e51.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=815209434473234709&skey=@crypt_c5903577_3de2ba57d9640c4c6b565940bdcad889&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1767445639486-4423b430-a8df-4108-a05d-8de1623b84b3.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

沈阳市出租车最新配色统一为波浪形上白下黄，但早期配色种类丰富，建议记忆顶灯样式。车侧一般都贴有椭圆形贴纸。

##### 2.大连市

- 品牌以大众和一汽为主

![3bbccea550977dd3685dde73fc628dc.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/jpeg/42695345/1720356049686-0ee5ada8-db9a-4b57-879f-06d3c577c8ab.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_23%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![5671d6a6990abfa081db77736db2e67.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/jpeg/42695345/1720356076199-180c6eff-1e0d-4794-84ae-a39979794272.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_29%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![7a684a3f0874d3174b6e3d32317df88.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/jpeg/42695345/1720356105233-d33a0230-5b17-4501-b1eb-379a9429b0cb.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_24%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

*xx式：指车型和配色均与某典型城市相似，且二者难以分辨

![1c6fc8fd11e3d5361b6a38f227711e0.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/jpeg/42695345/1720356139455-c323fa6f-5997-4b09-a6ca-2683bc2f24e9.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_27%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

大连市出租车大多是青银配色，只有少量白底绿线条配色。前车牌上方有着蓝色圆弧小牌子，易与天津、昆明等市出租车区分。

##### 3.鞍山市

- 以起亚赛拉图（图一）、大众捷达（图二图三）和现代伊兰特（图四青绿）为主

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738403380794-bc80970d-82ba-4c5c-b802-ab450aa2636e.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_31%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738403407308-2213220e-8e44-4ccc-8a1e-7a9faa9ec828.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_27%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738403431509-180747b2-da38-4893-9c8f-53fd72e76afc.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_27%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738403486797-419ceb07-d766-4f49-9153-965d3b771207.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_23%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

鞍山市出租车配色型号较为统一，有深绿、青绿（区别不大）和红银三种配色，且车身涂装较有特色，易于辨认。

##### 4.抚顺市

- 主要为铃木羚羊（图一图二），有少量其他车型（如图三）

![9965589b7c6910af4d0e8e683651e900.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759587854404-7108d489-1257-4c12-bfbc-938dd219b42f.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![6757ffb023ee76fbcb5f3e27aa0d010b.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759587863785-6801c4cd-74e2-4280-8e11-4b4a2dcb63c9.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![49e118ffb89d2ac81e9cd6d4424574a1.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759587922173-11cdfd19-94e7-460d-bdd6-8125b045f064.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_27%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

抚顺市出租车配色统一为上青下银，车型也较有特色。

##### 5.本溪市

- 主要为大众捷达（图一）和一汽威志（图二）

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=5444486533959736998&skey=@crypt_c5903577_4cfd908b196661c18808151dbab401c8&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769925461712-2c06d06b-0737-4039-9281-136b91703470.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=1129186930032640538&skey=@crypt_c5903577_4cfd908b196661c18808151dbab401c8&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769925471006-b2923c60-376e-42ef-9ca1-9796db08e5c9.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=2983094714943010005&skey=@crypt_c5903577_4cfd908b196661c18808151dbab401c8&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769925480990-bf7f6eb9-6503-46f4-9da1-72a24a23da8b.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

本溪市出租车型号配色较为统一，车侧印字均为白色，车前后的绿色圆弧小牌子也是其特点。

#### 河北省

##### 1.石家庄市

- 主要为大众捷达（图一图二）和现代伊兰特（图三），有部分起亚福瑞迪（图四）和北汽U5（图五）

![886b916b0dfbdcea40714e77ded193e3.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759827044749-c8aa2847-62f8-468f-8e8a-473a7381f030.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![35a46bf3c9d4b9e9038404177fa5f41f.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759827102283-10a8f0a7-b275-4088-b12b-44ef828fbb7e.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![000c511321ee958ec1681acc9596a1b2.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1763876527737-8aafb094-8fd0-479f-a19d-f8ead433bd8f.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

石家庄市出租车型号配色较为统一，且顶灯一般都有“石家庄”字样。

石市伊兰特和北京市的有些相似，但二者顶灯不同，后者结构更为简单。石市车侧为印字而非贴纸

##### 2.唐山市

- 大多为现代，如伊兰特（图一）和悦动（图二），以及部分广汽埃安S（图三）

![e644dec7b948713b1a49b632e066bfa.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/jpeg/42695345/1720357235972-5e2e0a29-ce2c-48aa-8547-dc148212c435.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_22%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![df201c7abe63eae1bc1aefebbb973ea.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/jpeg/42695345/1720357254641-b3fedb28-fd73-4c03-9dbc-35679d625652.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![6f30ebdde5303a5a08c0503d3d1c1c5.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/jpeg/42695345/1720357269853-b404a641-4ec3-4a8c-9e64-a59a546bf85c.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

唐山市出租车配色较为统一，分为蓝橙和蓝白两种。蓝白配色仅在埃安上出现。

北京、石家庄出租车与其相似，如遇请在题目中寻找其它线索进行辨别

##### 3.秦皇岛市

- 大多为大众捷达/桑塔纳（图一），有部分起亚福瑞迪（图二）和现代悦动（图三）

![28cc4b69b78715e1eb4f1f4040ba69ff.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759588334164-aef562a8-eac1-4e61-904e-2734838f3cf2.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_30%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![fcce25595ce3c52a4811fa516fe6468e.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759588343869-2d0de562-73eb-4201-9cc5-2ef927a9a30e.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![30ee63d666d214a186ce3418c26778c0.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759588358088-980e14a8-a2e5-446c-af3f-ed23533fe56f.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_31%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

秦皇岛市出租车配色统一为上青下银，车侧的蓝色贴纸是其重要特点，这有助于和天津、大连等城市做区分。

##### 4.邯郸市

- 主要为大众捷达/桑塔纳（除图二）和现代悦动（图二）

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=2658191662460163491&skey=@crypt_c5903577_4cfd908b196661c18808151dbab401c8&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769925977374-2c2ec711-d1aa-494b-8c45-c971637f38c4.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=4178970603133616024&skey=@crypt_c5903577_4cfd908b196661c18808151dbab401c8&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769925968352-66b4f431-6dd1-4fa1-93f4-a5a5b9d8327b.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=1842666428884178646&skey=@crypt_c5903577_4cfd908b196661c18808151dbab401c8&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769926043087-cd7bbd45-553a-4b28-9333-df5697d9bef5.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=2675065725193811614&skey=@crypt_c5903577_4cfd908b196661c18808151dbab401c8&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769926098231-12f1fd12-08ec-42c1-a63b-a86f7243bf63.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

邯郸市出租车中绿银配色数量最多，通常在车侧贴有圆形贴纸。其他配色则多在顶灯或车侧贴纸上印有“邯郸”字样。

##### 5.保定市

- 主要为长城C30（图一、二），有少量其他车型（如图三）

![5352827583e80ffd082d92b6e0325750.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759241375703-bbe988cc-2bc9-4407-be25-e98dff9011a1.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_30%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![05967e3f6783bade5cab61dde21f12c9.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759241397593-ef282a7b-9562-40d8-b0b8-f1046e5521cb.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_28%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![d6890c3b76ffb97e7dc99b526f6e699.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/jpeg/42695345/1720358351833-1105e2fb-08af-4042-b265-55752a21419b.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

- 特色车型 欧拉iQ

![06a50a58b846f86cb359a85adef7908b.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759241435907-acb9d11a-09b6-4e66-bf0c-9da180cd8017.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![4a30785aa903cc7c8f79389b0e623da9.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759241456570-ff8027dd-6e79-4202-bba0-2e271a232e56.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

保定市出租车配色统一为上红下银，车型也有特色，较好辨认。

保定市作为长城汽车公司总部所在地，街景中能看见大量长城牌汽车（包括旗下品牌如 欧拉）。欧拉iQ在该市能见度非常高（外地能见度较低，但石家庄数量也很多），且将其用作网约车服务。

#### 山西省

##### 1.太原市

- 早期以大众捷达/桑塔纳（图三）、三菱蓝瑟（图四）为主，最新车型统一为比亚迪E6

![default.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1763216030912-49394ed7-b795-48a2-9c9c-284dffd15455.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=9002499948640685014&skey=@crypt_c5903577_9cdf616dce07fe104f98e11e7e71a74d&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1763216155220-e66e77f2-1421-4c1f-8338-47308f4473f3.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=8719882545448951754&skey=@crypt_c5903577_9cdf616dce07fe104f98e11e7e71a74d&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1763216285805-96df6b9a-089f-4468-966b-b0e77278bd74.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=791022736821997230&skey=@crypt_c5903577_9cdf616dce07fe104f98e11e7e71a74d&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1763216300766-8cd9c3ec-85da-420b-b1b3-0efb543202f3.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

太原市出租车早期配色为银顶红身（且在山西省较为常见），后统一为波浪形蓝白相间的E6。

深圳(等地)比亚迪E6出租车与其相似，但两座城市环境特征有明显差异，较好分辨

##### 2.大同市

- 车型种类较多，品牌以大众、雪铁龙、起亚、吉利为主

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738319857436-b2523122-5e44-4d39-8744-cb0a143bdd5a.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_29%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738319906627-c665ed63-cf8d-4f18-bb73-22026da2a281.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738319964672-685c5869-dd61-4683-ac0c-89c6e0ba12a8.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738320032340-977edd53-c02d-4254-aecb-976aa93f4e84.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_28%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738320089933-f9e5db5c-5b80-4bd8-8bb3-4b95b90c868c.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_29%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738320127111-8619688f-b579-4212-bcc2-72b23340f8b1.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_25%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

大同市出租车配色大多为红银和蓝白，其他配色能见度较低。两种红银车的车侧基本都有着方形叫车贴纸，而两种蓝白车涂装特征明显（波浪形分色和祥云）。

##### 3.阳泉市

- 基本上为大众桑塔纳/捷达（除图二）

![d2e26b3113548c794337a559a41acd46.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759588826038-48320665-bf53-463e-a329-479c34ad7663.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![18c345723d3dd54819ee18564dc71585.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759588843911-755471c7-90f3-45c1-80bb-9676e2683325.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![57b4e53e4c9a24c48b250977a315b13c.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759588859238-0b80a4b3-b201-4ca6-a516-61f267b76004.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

阳泉市出租车型号配色都较为统一，且银顶红色车身很有特色，方便记忆。

##### 4.长治市

- 基本上为起亚赛拉图

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=4555934859083261960&skey=@crypt_c5903577_4cfd908b196661c18808151dbab401c8&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769926589046-3e3fe848-519c-4ddc-9ada-2a22c33d031b.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_18%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=7816210603906229065&skey=@crypt_c5903577_4cfd908b196661c18808151dbab401c8&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769926600182-b7ab9447-92e2-4aee-80c0-5c07e3478a00.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

长治市出租车型号配色统一，车侧的方形贴纸是其醒目特点。

##### 5.晋中市

- 基本上为大众桑塔纳（图一、三、四）和铃木尚悦（图二图五）

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=8376731287826658416&skey=@crypt_c5903577_d444a6425a1580bddfadc202b63c5877&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1775275662815-97f18ce1-dcab-4325-9b06-edaf5b14af08.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=4475778096214610022&skey=@crypt_c5903577_d444a6425a1580bddfadc202b63c5877&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1775275219727-bfe481b3-fa2b-4c22-b3a5-dc27bbafdb1b.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738408686617-67baf67d-736a-4fc9-bd01-c1f2f7d2f8a7.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_29%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738408701456-3e28fb0e-25cc-4ee5-8d0b-989b68c44507.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_27%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=7487286406784067315&skey=@crypt_c5903577_d444a6425a1580bddfadc202b63c5877&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1775275302362-e5adff25-a81f-4c4a-9e5f-63713af7c7dc.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

晋中市出租车早期配色较多，后期配色统一为蓝银（能见度最高），但车型保持不变。

​

#### 陕西省

##### 1.西安市

- 早期主要为比亚迪F3（图一）和少数比亚迪E6，有部分雪铁龙爱丽舍（图二），新的为比亚迪E5（图三）和吉利帝豪（图四）

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=3600210165459513882&skey=@crypt_c5903577_71a568fb45ef211da85e5f63a09e12ae&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769609744707-52596b69-0773-4442-964a-77310f666b9d.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_29%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=6828156253261979994&skey=@crypt_c5903577_71a568fb45ef211da85e5f63a09e12ae&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769609966731-e34ec379-7cc7-4cf3-a7bd-1be75b380f99.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_36%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=7446635354850664103&skey=@crypt_c5903577_71a568fb45ef211da85e5f63a09e12ae&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769609788526-effe7411-d8e2-43a8-ad51-880912563a0a.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_25%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=8767431798300488367&skey=@crypt_c5903577_71a568fb45ef211da85e5f63a09e12ae&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769609826395-aad9d1e4-a207-42dc-a3c9-0bb9032846a7.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

西安市出租车车型配色较为统一，早期配色以绿橙相间为主，有部分绿银，新的则分为全绿和全橙两种。且顶灯均有“西安”字样，易于辨认。

##### 2.铜川市

- 铃木尚悦（图一图二）、起亚锐欧（图三图四）、起亚赛拉图（图五）和大众捷达共四款车型

![26ca854a014cf7bf84e93b5039d70455.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759832706736-aa4d5cd6-9b89-4001-b52e-ed33851292b4.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![ef845d2ce6c6929300beaff0f475ddc0.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759832716192-07b835d7-73c6-4322-952a-1452918cfe5d.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![57f7a7d0618274bc569fa2740c93bf33.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759832741887-87568460-b788-4f2f-bcae-0e0eb55c5a9f.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![ad80d91146f7b95c3e69915ba8ab751e.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759832783912-2e4feed8-beb3-4515-a8bc-8b66be9c89b9.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![9a61717e8a004b009144abf51f5b0a79.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759832791102-b62c771d-9e02-42fc-a479-55cced938489.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_30%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

铜川市出租车型号较为统一，上绿下银配色最为常见。

吴忠出租车配色与其相似，且车型选取有重合，如遇请在题目中寻找其它线索进行辨别

##### 3.宝鸡市

- 主要为吉利英伦sc715（图一）、大众桑塔纳（图二）和吉利帝豪（图三）

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738500652280-37437c78-ecec-4407-a604-1a5c69950883.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_17%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738500707444-6b4ad6db-81c1-4b17-8c38-5d7cfb73460e.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738500719691-9a695654-d242-450f-a2be-5778e36578b1.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738500914662-3703e225-e332-4be2-84a3-858f9b1236b1.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_18%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

宝鸡市出租车车型种类统一，且配色较有特色（但颜色深浅不一），易于记忆。

##### 4.咸阳市

- 早期以大众桑塔纳（图一）、雪铁龙富康为主。新出租车大多为比亚迪F3（图二图四）、大众捷达（图三），有少数比亚迪E5、雷丁秦星

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738504799743-23f08c99-384c-498b-be50-dfa458386190.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_22%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738504745028-af52da1a-c415-4cec-b5d9-5b9b829d1091.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_24%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738504760774-85b077dc-bd95-46c0-a9d6-c44b38eccfb8.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_23%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738504776595-9b57df57-780e-4e2a-b909-3a4ed2a14ff5.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738504814271-50d14109-2d20-4172-b708-86fbd8aa6ff5.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_27%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738504842752-4cfeb16f-e178-49a5-b2ec-4f7b03990dce.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

咸阳市出租车型号较有特色，白绿（能见度最高）和白蓝车引擎盖上均有圆形涂饰，具有很高的辨识度。

##### 5.渭南市

- 主要为铃木启悦（图一）、尚悦（图二）、比亚迪 F3（图三）和雪铁龙爱丽舍四款车型

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=3787424239930287538&skey=@crypt_c5903577_4cfd908b196661c18808151dbab401c8&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769927014243-6d254fc8-4ec1-4368-90ea-55ff1d68425c.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=4704547739350795829&skey=@crypt_c5903577_4cfd908b196661c18808151dbab401c8&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769927032912-8664a314-29a4-4164-86e0-fb104c537dac.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=3802220345546399233&skey=@crypt_c5903577_4cfd908b196661c18808151dbab401c8&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769927024528-d455ca4b-e74e-4741-ab4d-6b50f4e85781.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

渭南市出租车配色统一为蓝橙相间，且车型也较有特色，易于辨认。

#### 宁夏回族自治区

##### 1.银川市

- 主要为大众桑塔纳（图一图三）和现代索纳塔（图四）

![IMG_20250808_200439.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754654869227-e34364c4-fce7-4f61-a683-77f928d6d795.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/jpeg/35193536/1707735941016-2712530a-8516-4a70-85a7-d55f537d06d1.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_27%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![IMG_20250808_200709.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754654896162-4005a46e-a768-4a84-b7a2-61d06ab6e426.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/jpeg/35193536/1707735941381-34797a2a-f94d-4e6f-acc7-46a8ff958d8a.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_28%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

​

银川市出租车有蓝黄和绿黄两种配色，较为统一。

##### 2.石嘴山市

- 主要为大众桑塔纳（图一）

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1749271504876-ee4f61d8-3ca2-4d98-b66e-683e1378704a.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1749271749222-8d3166e5-c41f-4e3c-8639-cc79456e8d84.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_22%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

石嘴山市出租车统一为红底黄带配色，有较高辨识度。

##### 3.吴忠市

- 大多为起亚赛拉图（图一图二）和铃木尚悦（图三）

![bbad3be2fea8bd26965b2f525c7b4c5.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1749273418384-103140b9-dfc1-4cc3-be88-4cf33d021962.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_31%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![021a938eab9423aebc9ea4288630f27.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1749273443034-ad9bc231-2955-4a02-af1e-6af8bc414e74.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_30%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![fc40149e32896a6345d1a6bb34fd849.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1749273449246-90b1e7e3-1e9b-4925-abdd-7dba467c6bc4.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

吴忠市出租车配色和车型较为统一，车侧圆形贴纸是其特点，这有助于区分西宁、铜川和宜春等地出租车。

##### 4.固原市

- 车型种类较多，其中现代瑞纳（图一）、铃木羚羊（图二图五）和比亚迪F3（图三）居多

![cfe709f1102348f8b5dfa28e960ced6d.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759834390105-59d6d50f-60d0-4431-a4fa-d10dad0b9391.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![a95a4a507b4b5dc2457890f66e5b6788.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759834406720-03ffea97-a1cd-430d-b692-141f1748f23e.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![514074a8b1568faa7a979fb8fa1790b9.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759834431475-ce1badd0-dfbc-4aae-ab6a-4bec71acf2d4.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![d035ab80249339b41b417d5cb490bb13.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759834525863-e0fb4bfd-499f-4fbd-8402-f4a5f743af66.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![fe18fb203e1b5fcc33938d715b0529f6.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759834534397-b30a5ca2-e6f8-4c57-8340-b9ccf4e9a7b4.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

固原市出租车配色和首府银川相同，也分为蓝黄和绿黄两种。但在车型选取上较有特色，且车侧贴纸上有“宁D（固原）”字样，部分车前方配有绿色圆弧小牌子。

固原出租车的黄带与银川相比更窄一些

##### 5.中卫市

- 以大众桑塔纳（图一）和铃木羚羊（图二）为主

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=158660000762516096&skey=@crypt_c5903577_656e2261e5a0723a79d2513098803f16&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1770380781017-5135ff15-c9fe-4f66-9aac-48f117678d24.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=1864385696845683615&skey=@crypt_c5903577_656e2261e5a0723a79d2513098803f16&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1770380790938-f380ada3-3906-493f-b784-230ab70c4f77.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_18%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

中卫市出租车配色统一为全黄，且均在车侧印有黑色字体的公司名称和“12328”运政服务热线，辨识度较高。

​

#### 甘肃省

##### 1.兰州市

- 品牌以北汽、吉利为主

![eedea3286e77f79bf0fa58afd95f86f3.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1763876873442-dd721934-a871-49c1-8d31-c799c9ee42c3.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

以上是其部分车型及配色

兰州市出租车型号涂装样式极其丰富。但大多都能在顶灯发现“兰州”字样。最好在出租车的基础上寻找题目中更多信息来定位兰州市。

##### 2.嘉峪关市

- 车型种类较多，多为现代（图一图二）

![6861ef4f6c57b2c82c26b68eb7cf727.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1749274612053-36b4daa0-c943-418f-b71d-c86c86951666.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_22%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![bf5dc5fd3df243c95ee6dd823d2a7c3.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1749274619292-d4088c73-8ae5-4faf-8d4c-940bdb336f3c.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_22%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![99acf88ae96b720e0d63e4fd18b3bba.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1749274633746-34a8eeda-cef1-4830-93e1-71fab8391f6c.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

嘉峪关市出租车配色统一为蓝底黄带，但黄带在车前后都延伸至底部，是醒目特征。

##### 3.金昌市

- 基本上是大众朗逸（图一至三），早期为铃木羚羊（图四）

![76b5493a320217173154c2cabfb4c28.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1749278357611-0abb19ac-9198-415b-8ce5-127553b22beb.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_28%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![7e9e534d5c463626833cbb6abcdebb8.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1749278367302-b0cf93da-7091-44dc-91f7-72321d96e6ff.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![d375fce269f44ac37cba5a9e7b3d7d7.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1749278440972-04456fff-545a-4659-b913-b3762693b9ee.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![75b99b8b50c4bbffe5c7153b0359034.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1749278452672-fccd6378-826d-4071-ab76-9bf7eb9e3663.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_31%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

金昌市出租车无论是旧还是新街景中配色和车型都很统一，车尾车侧有其车牌号印刷，且大多数都不会被打码，这有助于迅速锁定金昌市。

##### 4.白银市

- 主要为老桑塔纳（图一至四）和吉利全球鹰远景（图五图六）

白银市出租车配色十分丰富，但车型较有特点。通常在车侧印着蓝色的车牌号码（甘D）。

##### 5.天水市

- 全黄   铃木启悦（与重庆出租车高度相似！但重庆车顶灯竖放，天水车正常横向安装）

- 深绿银   现代伊兰特

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=2446153679888143206&skey=@crypt_c5903577_656e2261e5a0723a79d2513098803f16&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1770387747734-5cb58747-4d0c-4393-9829-bacfd6c532e4.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

天水市出租车型号配色种类丰富，以上是其详细分类。一般在车侧印着车牌号码（甘E），方便定位。

#### 新疆维吾尔族自治区

##### 1.乌鲁木齐市

- 多为大众捷达/桑塔纳（图一、四至七）以及雪铁龙爱丽舍（图二），有部分其他车型（如图三图八）

乌鲁木齐市出租车型号配色种类较多，涂装为全红的能见度较高。尽管不好记忆，但它仍然是区分乌市和新疆其他城市的一个好办法。

##### 2.昌吉州

★ ​昌吉市

- 主要为大众捷达/桑塔纳（除图三）和日产轩逸（图三）

昌吉州出租车型号配色较为统一，部分车侧贴有蓝色长方形贴纸。

昌吉绿银出租车与白银市的相似，前者多有蓝色贴纸或无涂饰，而后者一般为特色图案+印字

博乐市出租车型号配色较为统一，且车身简洁，较好辨认。

伊宁市出租车中红银和蓝银配色数量较多，车侧印字通常为弧形。

#### 内蒙古自治区

##### 1.呼和浩特市

- 大多为大众捷达（图一图三）和现代伊兰特（图二图四）

呼和浩特市出租车共有四种配色，但都有和北京市出租车同样的横橙带涂装，车身上的“12328”交通热线是明显特征。

##### 3.乌海市

- 大多为起亚锐欧（图一图二），有少量其他车型

![743d428d5ee4e43dd608961040c0fb6.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1749284431916-f48b427e-706d-4091-884e-a0c111ea71eb.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_17%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

乌海市出租车配色较为统一，大部分为青银配色，有少量红银配色，且车型具有特点。

##### 4.赤峰市

- 品牌以一汽、夏利和雪铁龙为主

赤峰市出租车型号配色较为统一，车侧贴纸通常为红色的字和边框。

##### 5.呼伦贝尔市

- 车型种类较多，其中大众捷达（图一前）、一汽威志 V5 和日产阳光（图三）居多

呼伦贝尔市出租车配色统一且涂装样式较为独特，易于辨认。

#### 青海省

##### 1.西宁市

- 主要为丰田花冠（图一图二）和大众桑塔纳（图三），有部分其他车型

西宁市出租车统一为上绿下银配色，车侧多有蓝色印刷字。

吴忠出租车与其相似，但二者绿色深浅程度、车侧贴纸不同，如遇请仔细观察

##### 2.海东市

- 多为大众捷达（图一图二）

![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1749285643819-27d04e8d-c251-47c4-a04c-5c7d9770b78a.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fformat%2Cwebp%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_17%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![653058e287f0d18076d02f3cc7f603b.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1749285658234-cd83662d-ea2b-48b4-901c-be36b3678738.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_18%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![41ca62779b25c2700217ad459cdfe10.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1749285669420-a2f7b102-7971-491f-887f-7eecde0ccfcd.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

海东市出租车配色统一为绿银，车侧有白色印刷字，这对区分省会西宁十分重要。

海东出租车相对西宁来说车型更老旧

#### 西藏自治区

##### 1.拉萨市

- 早期为现代索纳塔（图一）和中华尊驰（图二）两款车型。新出租车主要为大众朗逸（图三图四），有部分斯柯达明锐（图五）和卡罗拉双擎（图六）

拉萨市出租车型号配色较为统一，且富有西藏本土特色，很好辨认。

##### 2.昌都市

- 主要为大众桑塔纳（图一图二)和雪铁龙世嘉（图三）

昌都市出租车配色统一为蓝橙，车侧贴纸印有昌都字样，易于辨认。

##### 3.山南市

- 基本上为大众桑塔纳（下图均是）

![b46dffa4515fc9ea021b702d5f08566.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1752473130396-36ae3eff-2545-4166-ac80-ce253c71a951.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![9f0d681886f252c433b60a6c976e5e9.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1752473153328-b8759359-89c1-46e5-9c3e-b888280df173.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

山南市出租车型号配色统一，车门一般印有两行白色文字。

##### 4.日喀则市

- 为大众桑塔纳（图二至四）和现代悦动（图一）两款车型

日喀则市出租车型号统一，且配色较有特点，易于辨认。

##### 5.那曲市

- 统一为大众桑塔纳（下图均是）

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=7637185325282662020&skey=@crypt_c5903577_656e2261e5a0723a79d2513098803f16&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1770389162058-601bd19f-6ce7-47a0-bfbf-beeebe952e06.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=5362307218290475472&skey=@crypt_c5903577_656e2261e5a0723a79d2513098803f16&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1770389177902-d850ab5a-0a6b-4429-b41a-63f906f12ae8.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=517843715205391992&skey=@crypt_c5903577_656e2261e5a0723a79d2513098803f16&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1770389186310-34887fb6-2e5f-4516-b607-da3bb55f162e.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

那曲市出租车共有两种白绿涂装，且都富有地域特色，极易辨认。

#### 四川省

##### 1.成都市

- 基本上为大众捷达（图一图五），新能源车有吉利帝豪ev Pro（图二）、东风风神E70（图三）和帝豪ev450（图四）三款车型

![6cfe9edaafb4c4f0bcdfc37ffdc1bb5b.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759828133951-3852c575-d5a4-486b-8ba5-2ab3a6f94668.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![c497e0f3f8ea4f8b0d844fc72887418c.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759828148938-6d7a68fb-3923-4664-aad2-264b1bdfe16b.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![fe699e338ed76f35aa84151f0c19246d.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759828160522-a7725f1e-927a-4f67-9560-653b6aee903f.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![9b463bdb573e84f845a305cda49e137d.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1759828169274-d551435a-73b5-4380-b0c2-a3d51bea5c15.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/jpeg/35193536/1707735951957-338c30e3-4d33-41b7-afc5-ae57074e3672.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

​

成都市出租车型号配色较为统一，车侧的公司名称和编码通常为黄色，引擎盖上多印有“太阳神鸟”城市形象标志或大熊猫，易于辨认。

##### 2.绵阳市

- 品牌大多为大众、雪铁龙和中华

![0c9ef055554fad4161ac7ac2fab948b.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1752474684665-43bcccf9-5906-4d57-bcb2-d3d032fdd796.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![a4d97d34b91a992173626d3012d00ff.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1752474695257-3f009dc7-2e1b-4a64-9446-a509ed450820.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![6208117c3850347a97f7e5c027b4857.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1752474707109-c9fed759-dc44-48f9-89fa-9470124e403e.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

绵阳市出租车配色种类较多，其中前三种配色能见度较高。

##### 3.自贡市

- 基本上为大众宝来

![f9315d285a1f556a57614627f177627.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1752476288523-578a6b04-b7df-4840-abd4-46396625f0f2.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_15%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![2dba443928de0a4057d910eecfdb2ec.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1752476299293-a1d3ff42-00a0-45fb-97bb-46ad2fc09f7c.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![b5ecec691d2e664c32631eb4599bd97.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1752476309124-ed50fb2f-cd88-449e-83c5-cd87dd61f4ff.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_18%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

自贡市出租车配色统一为上绿下银，引擎盖上印有恐龙图案，且车门印有醒目黄色字，较好辨认。

##### 4.攀枝花市

- 基本上为大众桑塔纳

![859c7beda120079ff08ac1753afe4490.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1763878593861-d7f6558c-1e66-4464-98d6-67afc8215f66.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![3e82072c9de2362002132ce1f0f8cd1b.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1763878605008-67f581c9-ce8e-4f8a-982a-341e76aa8c4f.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![14a85658cb13ea1810663a0849c3b30d.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1763878688086-11834961-405a-4d13-b7b0-f228c85f7ced.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![601d6ce7de6ac8e69d5e073119160b6a.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1763878695662-a2a488ec-0f05-47e5-b142-2c19ead6e20b.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

攀枝花市出租车型号配色统一，通常在车侧印着白色四位编号和公司名称，易于记忆。

##### 5.泸州市

- 主要为大众捷达（图一图三）和宝来（图二），有少量比亚迪 E6

泸州市出租车型号配色较为统一，车侧贴纸也有特色，易于辨认。

#### 云南省

##### 1.昆明市

- 多为大众捷达/桑塔纳（图一、二、四），有部分其他车型

![d936240ac6c10ec8ba6a10e5370694c9.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1763877990865-7f0f0060-0252-44b0-8e87-867a30be32ac.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![9f120e5dd8a9691db56f70080e3aef56.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1763878005180-90cbc14b-bb22-4bea-b121-4cf526c33d38.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

- 云能行网约车

![eb48491d3dd13b8ef507b5c3cbed3779.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1763878141304-5e018a16-325a-40a9-bc27-5ade3aa166a7.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

昆明市出租车型号配色较为统一，部分配色颇具云南色彩，较有特点。

天津市出租车也是青银配色，但二者顶灯不同，天津市结构简单无电子显示屏

##### 2.昭通市

- 主要为大众宝来（图一图二）

![0cb86430a5034dbf029ba2d4969732a.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1752479535599-accc3b0c-96cf-419e-9a5c-da307e9d4236.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_16%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![a495d458e1134f4d1ac0307580e9d0b.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1752479546413-cb2db13f-1f04-4237-aed6-a0f258d9f668.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![1b3fc9b3be36a788db4153236b2f9c4.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1752479558428-e0ca55ea-8534-40d9-aac7-fc3d56c74265.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

昭通市出租车型号配色较统一。昭通是黑颈鹤的故乡，因此多在车侧印有黑颈鹤图案，易于辨认。

##### 3.曲靖市

- 主要为起亚赛拉图（除图四）

![f1d1d0622948c06944746d4a03ca77e.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1752480595555-14c774bb-2c56-491d-bc4f-b213b811e20f.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![b1d88435c4bf54fd8a11adc2a8b7003.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1752480610256-181c5b89-a850-4498-96d1-66debd62d181.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![d5dc43fca78ac00f289c2b3c9a62c54.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1752480622538-31529d12-f123-47f2-9102-fff9c850f5c7.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![95d2da44f9f92cb489ab5fa5a2d252b.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1752480632832-fd28587d-ceab-4527-860f-0f220f75d967.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_18%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

曲靖市出租车配色统一且较有特点，为波浪形上黄下绿，极易辨认。

##### 4.楚雄州

★ 楚雄市

- 基本上为大众捷达/桑塔纳（图一图二）和雪铁龙爱丽舍（图三）

![58f47642365e32f545d8be104d9b0810.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1764337220678-f58ae248-0dd2-4d1e-a0a3-3524efe176eb.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![e699af4fc49adec23adcbc0f9144de45.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1764337231688-379951b7-af32-448a-b0c7-8881d9e0cbd5.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![27523a3b94fad81b9a24fa5083d8d5cf.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1764337241858-8d180ee4-ba66-4045-b6b7-876b973baf10.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

楚雄市出租车型号配色较为统一，且涂装贴纸富有本地特色，较好辨认。

玉溪市出租车型号统一，顶灯通常印有”玉溪“字样，方便定位。

六盘水市出租车型号配色较为统一，蓝橙、白蓝配色能见度较高。

遵义市出租车主要有四种配色，其中白蓝能见度较高。车侧多印着“遵义“字样，易于辨认。

- 以起亚赛拉图（图一图五）、现代伊兰特（图二）和雪铁龙爱丽舍（图四）为主

铜仁市出租车型号较统一，但配色略显平庸，通常在车侧印着“12328”交通热线。如遇请结合题中其他信息进行定位。

兴义市出租车型号配色较为统一，易于记忆。

![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/jpeg/35193536/1707735957630-7c024a1b-7575-456b-9451-ae07f958befe.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_29%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

​

![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/jpeg/35193536/1707735958034-409673b5-09f5-4088-bcbe-e9a7f00a3c1b.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_30%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

​

南宁市出租车型号较为统一，配色种类丰富但通常下底为银色，且顶灯均有“南宁”字样。有些车侧贴着“95128”交通热线的四边形贴纸。

##### 2.柳州市

- 品牌以现代为主，有少量其他车型

柳州市出租车配色种类十分丰富，其中大多都是橙色下车身。车侧贴纸也较有特点。

##### 3.桂林市

- 主要为铃木启悦（图一 仅有全红配色）和大众捷达（图二、三、五），有部分现代和比亚迪

桂林市出租车配色及车型种类丰富，全红、银黄绿配色车数量最多。部分车头左前方处配有绿色圆弧小牌子。

##### 4.梧州市

- 车型种类较多，其中海马海福星（图一）、铃木尚悦（图三）和羚羊（图四）居多

梧州市出租车配色较为统一，且具有较高的辨识度。车侧印字多为弧形，易于记忆。

##### 5.北海市

- 基本上为大众桑塔纳（下图均是）

北海市出租车型号配色较为统一，且顶灯通常印有“北海”字样，车侧的三块蓝色贴纸也是其特点，易于辨认。

#### 山东省

##### 1.济南市

- 早期主要为大众朗逸（图一）和捷达/桑塔纳（图二）。新的车型种类较多，以新能源车为主

![be2c768881102c9d6c0d25c64029f86b.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1764340184679-b1e6b152-15c2-4e91-8776-23965409c318.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![15ec1c5dcafe00a3b9b49c632285a72f.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1764340281679-a7662858-3dc3-44f0-97ba-e894c4d74098.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

济南市出租车前后期配色虽有变化但不太明显，车侧贴纸及其荷花图案较有特色，易于辨认。

早期配色与昆明市、天津市相似，天津市顶灯独特，昆明市车侧仅印公司名称无贴纸

##### 2.青岛市

- 品牌以大众为主（除后两张），黑色礼宾车有斯柯达速派（图七）、雪铁龙C5（图八）和大众帕萨特三种

![7cd1c8432c9648d2faf8bdaed0e1394.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754482338543-4d7bfdd2-593e-4de3-95b0-89456febed92.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![ccdd7c656dcabb39a3a34e7c3a128f7.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754482348908-446b8465-6926-4343-ba96-85b0b71da9f7.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

青岛市出租车虽配色种类较多，但通常下底为银色（类似南宁出租车），车侧青岛专属“Q”样标志是醒目特点，易于辨认。

##### 3.淄博市

- 品牌以大众和起亚为主

![51326a3ca63fdabf58ae98bf550ad2d.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754483809529-1ae37450-4d40-417e-87a6-821479c6e994.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![5ccabcb88bf6da1daec45c34c3f9f8e.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754483821635-3d3e93db-73a3-4c57-86d2-9bf17644bff1.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_30%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![b9656610085785c28d3214fcde916d9.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754483833489-9a699a76-9732-4c06-ab2f-991bd4985aa3.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_28%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

淄博市出租车配色统一为上青下银，且顶灯均有“淄博”字样，较好辨认。

##### 4.枣庄市

- 统一为大众桑塔纳（下图均是）

![6bc2dbeb9613bcc966c96aeae92225db.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1764341689801-22ee17ff-7497-4a72-9fc3-eca6f6734596.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![fd564832eb7c9c5f36cadee787ff776a.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1764341698307-9050ed0a-70de-426d-9aef-3f1b1f2cd734.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![9e4b961e0b7e8e907000d76a109dba60.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1764341950117-580fd10b-c210-45e5-8751-2d02b6191c27.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![9d2b8b1868916248e66fc005fb967a2b.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1764341958312-413b858c-fed0-4115-ba58-bd31cb4e3169.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

枣庄市出租车型号配色较为统一，其中市中区为绿银配色，蓝/绿橙配色则出现于薛城区（市政府驻区）。

##### 5.东营市

- 早期主要为大众桑塔纳/捷达（图一图三）、现代伊兰特（图二）和中华骏捷 FSV（图四）三款车型。新车有北汽U5（图五左上） 铃木启悦（右上）  奇瑞艾瑞泽5（左下） 起亚福瑞迪（右下）和现代悦动五款车型

东营市出租车早期有两种配色，新车则保留蓝银配色，顶灯样式也发生变化。车侧贴纸形状与省会济南相同，较好辨认。

#### 河南省

##### 1.郑州市

- 旧出租车多为丰田花冠（图一）和大众桑塔纳（图二），新的主要为荣威Ei5（图三）、小鹏G3（图四）以及启辰D60ev（图五）

![e220bd5792c55b7bcd52f773f467f38f.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1764342482458-e4c4d79f-827a-4923-9103-48da76f3a58e.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![1ab03207edbedd7cf986d5a74d816ef1.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1764342490255-0ceed49f-1c8f-4798-8f74-7fd519c42613.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![532ad0525767ee004106425535777c40.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1764342660322-7c858f4f-4d88-43c1-884b-7e329fc8ba2b.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

郑州市出租车无论是旧版还是新版都采用绿银相间配色，且车型也较统一，很好辨认。

##### 2.开封市

- 大多为大众桑塔纳/捷达(图一图二）和奇瑞旗云3（图四），有部分其他车型。新车有长安逸动ev460（图五）、奇瑞艾瑞泽5e（图六）、比亚迪秦ev（图七）和江淮思皓e50A（图八）四款车型（均为绿牌新能源车。旧涂装仍使用)

![5c1cc26d56a8959de015d31338af504.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754630746421-aac05c59-ce41-4cf0-805d-0185975d349e.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![eedc33d7b96347c09fe1d2efaf3ea83.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754630777192-e802d3c9-b935-43c4-95f2-ebd4afe8b9be.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![2bd788a1406439d612e731da40519fb.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754630860452-0b922ac3-94af-4525-a1c0-865f2a2b376b.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

开封市出租车主要有两种配色，其中蓝白/银的涂装样式变种较多。新引入的四款车型较有特点，辨识度较高。

##### 3.洛阳市

- 主要为雪铁龙爱丽舍（图一）、大众桑塔纳（图二图五）和现代伊兰特（图四），新的为广汽埃安S（图七）和长安逸动ev460（图八）两款新能源车（旧涂装仍使用）

![f87233419d2e0391036596723f25931.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754636037311-99f8f147-0a8e-480c-ad5a-3a85dfb828f6.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_24%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![a59d320507c75312737dfdac74fd334.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754636044192-48462ca0-b4b6-4332-98d4-3d44361cb5e9.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![f8438226d4fb44bb01c83cef81c4ca3.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754636052841-e8ffd1c7-8dc9-4c9c-9f36-74479377371e.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_31%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![9d4e4e32285e96c63906ee618a0fcd0.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754636062482-de470dda-eba8-4beb-9cc2-4bbbbca31e83.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_29%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![a4ddc43e91dbb614899961c79726be4.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754636086233-28478bcd-8550-4e81-8c36-e899889a8f13.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

洛阳市出租车型号丰富，车侧的方形弧顶贴纸十分醒目，易于辨认。

洛阳新能源出租车与开封的相似，但后者下底部为白色，且车侧所印的“12328”为黑色或白色

##### 4.平顶山市

- 以大众捷达/桑塔纳（图二）、起亚赛拉图（图一图三）和锐欧（图四）为主

平顶山市出租车型号配色较为统一，易于记忆。

##### 5.安阳市

- 主要为大众桑塔纳（图一）和比亚迪E6（图三图四）

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=3113975528563621627&skey=@crypt_c5903577_df45c7f52226c977c404305e5ee02778&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1772284394841-26367d65-4f0c-40aa-9223-35ccfeef8d90.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=7463084156310305178&skey=@crypt_c5903577_df45c7f52226c977c404305e5ee02778&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1772284409043-b0de0f1c-3098-4c78-92e7-64e719ccaba0.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=9194472276425269187&skey=@crypt_c5903577_df45c7f52226c977c404305e5ee02778&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1772284467949-458820c0-a330-4531-99ab-6142ad4e2012.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=3463272123477216352&skey=@crypt_c5903577_df45c7f52226c977c404305e5ee02778&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1772284476682-5789a7e7-1ce8-400c-8ca2-42ad189384d2.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_31%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

安阳市出租车型号配色较为统一，大多在顶灯和车侧贴纸上印有“安阳”字样，易于定位。

安阳的比亚迪E6均为绿牌，且后挡风玻璃上贴有红底白字带。这些信息有助于您与太原、深圳等地作区分

#### 江苏省

##### 1.南京市

- 早期主要为大众桑塔纳和现代索纳塔。新的车型种类较多，其中现代悦动（图一)和大众朗逸（图二）居多，也有不少新能源车

南京市出租车型号种类丰富，但配色较为统一，旧街景中以上银下金配色为主（由于大部分被新街景覆盖，所以能见度较低），较新街景中全黄配色最为常见。车侧的圆形大贴纸很有特点，较好辨认。

重庆市黄色出租车在车型选取上与南京的没有重合，且二者顶灯不同，容易分辨

徐州市出租车型号配色较为丰富，绿银和蓝橙配色能见度较高，车侧的贴纸上均有“徐州市区”字样。

##### 4.常州市

- 主要为大众桑塔纳（图一图二），有部分其他车型（如图三）

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=789093919867733418&skey=@crypt_c5903577_41de410d6fb1980db9c016a23d4c0122&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1765100029453-c86be46e-b0d2-4ab4-affc-cf6328f88b13.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=4742341174310918518&skey=@crypt_c5903577_41de410d6fb1980db9c016a23d4c0122&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1765100051181-349f7760-3a29-4ba2-997a-b061b793988e.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=7582132415320117468&skey=@crypt_c5903577_41de410d6fb1980db9c016a23d4c0122&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1765100084777-82700943-37fe-408e-8d6e-e2168e693569.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

常州市出租车配色统一为上绿下银，车侧印字（公司名称和监督电话）通常靠近车把手，部分车顶灯有超大电子显示屏。

- 主要为大众桑塔纳（图一图四图五）和朗逸（图二），有部分其他车型

苏州市出租车中白银配色能见度最高，车侧通常印有“苏州”字样，且顶灯样式较为特别，易于辨认。

#### 安徽省

##### 1.合肥市

- 多为雪铁龙爱丽舍（图一）、大众桑塔纳（图二图七图八）和江淮牌（图三至五、图十），也有不少其他车型（如图六图九）

合肥市出租车中青绿银配色最为常见，并且其车尾处有银色带状点缀，部分车型也较有特点，易于辨认。顶灯形状特别且有“合肥”字样，背面的整形广告也是其特征，值得记忆。

##### 2.芜湖市

- 基本上为奇瑞旗云2（图一图二图七）、E3（图三至六、图九）和A5（图十），有少量其他车型（如图八）

芜湖市出租车型号及配色种类丰富，蓝橙、白橙配色能见度较高。大多都在车侧印着”W“状芜湖标志。

##### 3.蚌埠市

- 有大众桑塔纳（图一图二图六）、奇瑞A5（图三）和雪铁龙新旧爱丽舍（图四图五）

![278407755433d844a3d1d5be92442e5d.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756021447739-715f3ff2-14d0-4519-883a-adf4b5e476e6.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![3b984f5e7dd9a167fffe1ef24fc9267b.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756021455290-efbe91d0-066c-4f91-86b0-4afb6786163b.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![05319ef73f71fce3f145049ae58c7711.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756021464040-f723a599-87d3-4a6a-89f5-914a1ccde3e0.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![b2009566203c9e058bf0dff84d40aedf.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756021471314-b08f4b16-fc89-41c2-a7cb-c433d4eb9984.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![b70603744f047a0c76d383eda0eabe8f.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756021479951-4819da2c-d470-4d54-9c54-255a782e836d.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![2fb9f7b78ca44e537ef89659caa567e3.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756021489252-be262b97-dc49-49e4-8761-5192a7e464d3.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

蚌埠市出租车配色种类较多，其中蓝银数量最多。车侧通常印有其所属公司的名称，字体颜色为蓝色。

开封市蓝银变体与蚌埠的相似，但前者能见度较低，且车身所印文字均为黑色

##### 4.淮南市

- 以大众捷达/桑塔纳（图二图三）和奇瑞（图一图五）为主，有部分比亚迪 F3（图四）

淮南市出租车型号较为统一，其中绿橙/黄配色数量最多。车侧通常贴有绿色圆形贴纸，且顶灯形状较有特点，易于辨认。

##### 5.马鞍山市

- 主要为大众桑塔纳（图一)、起亚赛拉图（图二）和铃木启悦（图三）三款车型

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=9204800095643899072&skey=@crypt_c5903577_d444a6425a1580bddfadc202b63c5877&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1775275742670-f90f054c-64eb-4315-a1de-fd81e6a4b4e2.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

马鞍山市出租车配色统一为上红下银，车侧印字多为白色，较好辨认。

#### 湖北省

##### 1.武汉市

- 主要为雪铁龙爱丽舍（图一）、大众捷达（图二）和东风牌（图三 风神S30、图四 风神A60），也有不少其他车型，如东风风神E60（图五1）、别克微蓝6（图五2）、比亚迪秦EV（图五3）等。早期为雪铁龙旧爱丽舍和凯旋（图九后2）两款车型

武汉市出租车在较新街景中橙白相间配色数量最多，而且具有特点，易于辨认。但早期配色十分丰富（大部分被覆盖）。湖北省部分城市出租车与之相似，如遇请寻找其他信息仔细分辨。

- 主要为大众桑塔纳（图一图七）和雪铁龙新旧爱丽舍（图二至六）

黄石市出租车型号较为统一，配色中全青和全绿能见度最高。

##### 3.十堰市

- 主要为东风风神A60（图一）、风神S30（图二）和雪铁龙旧爱丽舍（图三）三款车型

![45a6f3c1e960df919a19a61108158cf1.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756029160171-d03c7558-9393-4dac-a0a4-debea50dc22a.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_30%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![e242e2cb783cecaf57424ca4b28f895f.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756029174758-264568fa-7cec-47be-b597-4cb492708618.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_27%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

十堰市出租车配色统一为银顶青色车身，且车型也较有特点，易于辨认。

##### 4.荆州市

- 主要为雪铁龙旧爱丽舍（图二至四），有部分其他车型（如图一）

荆州市出租车型号较为统一，车侧印字在青色车上为红色，在其他配色上为白色。

##### 5.宜昌市

宜昌市出租车配色统一且富有特色，易于记忆。

#### 湖南省

##### 1.长沙市

- 早期基本上是大众捷达/桑塔纳（图一至三），新的有吉利帝豪ev450（图四）、比亚迪秦ev（图五）和E5

![3d7c83140795cd0ddb46b35ca5229745.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756298512423-b6f22c4c-5394-4706-8b41-065ca708bb1e.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/jpeg/35193536/1707735967613-6f2e0b09-5683-4c05-aff8-186e2a1f1ee8.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_31%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![2ef02f069ecc28cd97c1de7a9dafe98b.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756293848643-b58c9337-3506-4c2c-9ef4-7fcc8105dc2e.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_31%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![b92e33eac0252989e2cb06ac3be36070.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756293870738-74378106-23f0-4b6b-ac0c-b17df914a03d.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_28%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

长沙市出租车早期也有蓝银配色，但仍以橙蓝和绿橙为主（湖南其他城市也有相似出租车）。后期配色统一为上蓝下银，且顶灯一般有“长沙”字样。车侧的星状贴纸是明显特征，便于与其他城市区分。

##### 2.株洲市

- 主要为现代伊兰特（图一）和悦动（图二），有少量北汽（图三图四）

![2176206b8587f2ba282b722f3b58e714.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756037635726-eaa0430f-f9fd-41db-8b21-5cd462855242.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![a3b14f3c35fcafe40740eef0a428fb78.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756037658069-550e3b62-2efb-495b-ab8a-f69de4ecdef8.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_31%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![69e0454b169d2ca6652dce1340d68da1.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756037646710-8d67a0af-f77a-4035-936f-256fc80b2447.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_28%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![a1135be23a676b0ac6894631a589ea9f.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756037665419-e80b4d58-e94b-4eed-8e07-68156e1316f5.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

株洲市出租车型号配色较为统一，大多数车身上有着黑色格点印花，或贴着蓝色贴纸。通常车尾有其车牌号和编号印刷。

##### 3.湘潭市

- 基本上为吉利远景（图一图二）和英伦sc715（图三），有部分大众桑塔纳（图四）和吉利帝豪ev450（图五）

![4ca796603271b27cc1a687e4a546bae0.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756038711614-8490e8ff-4d1f-43b0-a4f0-a1243023e415.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_28%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![d182bcf42adec0e7dc7653b4b3bd54a9.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756038729963-2647b642-4447-4d5c-8faa-dfccc6f39add.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![610c3ab0e3c99535ea121441eb808311.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756038740146-35dace89-ffe5-4ceb-b03d-ab480769b7fd.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![1530de4625ef821a1057c51ef31a48a9.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756081763368-cd76e1d3-0c55-4f28-9f95-3aa936238f85.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![bc0d1c9530a8359616348d62145b25e9.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756082055019-dd25b30f-41ce-4fe4-9414-5f572e0de02f.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_22%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![8b8d9d1bc2dfe466846565f9c060595d.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756039194484-8edb509b-f0d3-41f4-90af-873067cc0bbc.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_28%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

湘潭市出租车蓝橙配色数量最多，其他配色能见度较低，但车型选择得很有特色，易于辨认。

湘潭出租车的顶灯多有投放“点石家装”的广告，这有助于您更加确定目标地点为湘潭。但请注意，该方法仅为辅助手段，需与型号配色等信息结合使用，切勿只通过该方法确定位置。（石家庄这招太狠了

##### 4.衡阳市

- 主要为大众捷达/桑塔纳（图一至三、图六）和雪铁龙爱丽舍（图四图五）两款车型

衡阳市出租车型号较为统一，但部分配色与省会长沙相似，如遇请在题目中寻找其它线索辨别两地。

##### 5.邵阳市

- 基本上为大众桑塔纳（下图均是）

邵阳市出租车与湖南其它城市的高度相似，且配色种类较为丰富。大多在车尾印有车牌号码（这可能是区分他市的唯一特征）。如遇请在题目中寻找其它线索进行辨别。

南昌市出租车型号较统一，三种配色均有波浪形分色，车侧上印的公司、车牌号也很有特点，易于辨认。

##### 2.赣州市

- 主要为大众捷达/桑塔纳（图一至三），有少量现代伊兰特（图四图六）等其他车型
