![3afe271c54d15bc3bd1c8123798f9677.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756294784066-8d2d9a79-9ec1-49dd-8c07-78e095bec857.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_28%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![0783b7f72fd642617f27f6b1bfc54b4f.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756294486059-6fc2e1c5-7eb9-4149-a0ca-f6ceb1f30172.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_31%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![8976e7b88c42cddb40a584c2c29580b2.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756294573853-d28420ba-bd37-47c5-bdfa-a5b84330af31.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

赣州市出租车配色种类虽多但较有特色，车前方通常设有圆弧小牌子，车侧的贴纸和编号也较有特点。

##### 3.宜春市

- 以大众桑塔纳（图一图二）和现代伊兰特（图三）为主

![947904b78316a3f4d3f4240247b9cf17.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756299957067-c98a2d4f-9334-4aca-8dc9-b3e6f6e59f58.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_27%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![1f51f6b1f71932effe2f4641622282d2.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756299965221-7a409468-91bc-4310-bbd1-ab51391cf365.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_31%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![29cf82f19c1dd6a90c2e7f79897f9bc2.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756299973093-04ad7314-5b63-4af0-82b5-df9197595052.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_29%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![0a8cb157aeb664f9d600e295533dbfed.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756299984083-0a561c74-867c-4062-bc2f-aee1f611d0b8.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_28%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

宜春市出租车型号配色较为统一，且大多都在车侧贴着“12328”热线的方形贴纸。

洛阳、吴忠也有与宜春相同的绿银配色出租车，并且也在车侧贴有12328贴纸。但洛阳车的贴纸类似方形加弧顶，吴忠车则多有一个圆形贴纸

##### 4.吉安市

- 主要为日产轩逸（图一）和大众捷达/桑塔纳（图二至四）

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=5817311201343997394&skey=@crypt_c5903577_71a568fb45ef211da85e5f63a09e12ae&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769611265555-442f845a-1e40-4322-9833-5a5465ca4891.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=7643242483870823240&skey=@crypt_c5903577_71a568fb45ef211da85e5f63a09e12ae&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769611273412-4bed56be-8a23-449a-a1e5-211106cb9be2.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_31%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=3707889240512948772&skey=@crypt_c5903577_71a568fb45ef211da85e5f63a09e12ae&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769611284061-d9efaa6a-b835-425e-85be-af23eb752a10.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_31%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=2894906865375832615&skey=@crypt_c5903577_71a568fb45ef211da85e5f63a09e12ae&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1769611291940-61919288-3008-4487-a939-b1dc7bffbc7f.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

吉安市出租车型号较为统一，涂装样式也有特色，且大多在车顶和车侧印着车牌号，易于辨认。

吉安出租车配色与省会南昌相似，但二者在车型选取上基本无重合

##### 5.上饶市

- 主要为大众桑塔纳（图一），有少量其他车型

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=1642590852151985314&skey=@crypt_c5903577_d444a6425a1580bddfadc202b63c5877&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1775278991061-c52fb3ae-0237-4b08-b2a8-429a69bf06c5.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=1489599905374498353&skey=@crypt_c5903577_d444a6425a1580bddfadc202b63c5877&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1775279013664-4545d92e-1f12-4ad3-ae67-f808111f9290.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_30%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

上饶市出租车型号配色较为统一，一般在车侧印有“SR（上饶）”字样，较好辨认。

#### 浙江省

##### 1.杭州市

- 主要为现代索纳塔（图一图五图六）、悦动（图三）和日产轩逸（图二），也有部分其他车型

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=7662747311229369776&skey=@crypt_c5903577_41de410d6fb1980db9c016a23d4c0122&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1765100606444-f61a7b45-54e8-4f1e-a780-11de44ab3b33.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

杭州市出租车配色种类虽多但通常下底为银色，车侧西湖图案和黄色电子屏显顶灯是其特点，较好辨认。

##### 2.宁波市

- 早期以大众捷达/桑塔纳（图一至三）为主，新的主要为铃木启悦（图四）、大众朗逸（图六）和现代悦动。新能源车有比亚迪秦ev（图七）、长安逸动ev460（图八）和睿蓝枫叶60S（图九）三款车型

![d263b84c3ee93cccef7f84c3943757fe.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756303843023-a805b742-6ce8-4e11-976a-1f7c893ce1d3.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![3da953380cf1912383c19f5d2531699c.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756305222089-b42babcb-c4e0-4fe3-8816-0acbce238b5a.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_31%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![8f7d917925f2387aa9f3db8faff792a1.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756305230141-ed412dc1-aa63-416f-9d35-beaa51e3be22.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

宁波市出租车配色种类十分丰富，早期一般都以银色下底为主。新的蓝银配色居多，车侧还带有类似叶子的涂饰。引擎盖上大多都贴有圆形贴纸，且顶灯样式比较特别，易于辨认。

##### 3.温州市

- 大多为大众捷达/桑塔纳（图二图三）。新能源车中吉利帝豪ev450（图四）和帝豪ev Pro（图五）居多

![3a227700034492840cd5798760443f09.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756615368570-778593bf-a28d-494c-bd35-6035f1ea0625.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![86215b35ae5f00cb0bacaeb37c17764b.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756615374971-0f75dcb6-b024-42c9-80bc-90b63954efb4.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![42a0a7b73c1b03e893f84522e430e24d.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756615392829-d6fecdb9-d4ec-4980-b0bc-0492436a3288.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_32%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![06750d55ab9ee6618751f1b5e1d7a1fb.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756615405639-5b243cf1-b4aa-45be-a0a7-93aee2638847.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_31%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![b822f61e727613a8b0c35b15d190b395.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756615413800-6b2f22ef-b36c-4b0d-8007-c80e59637adb.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![7b6c0ad594edb92493e4993938affcd8.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756615424292-185d8437-208a-40f5-8b14-c7afe3a53c02.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

温州市出租车配色种类虽多但通常下底为银色，且波浪形分色较有特色。车侧温州特有丝带状图案易于辨认。

##### 4.绍兴市

- 以大众捷达/桑塔纳（图二图三）和现代悦动（图一）为主

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=1986655683045733651&skey=@crypt_c5903577_3de2ba57d9640c4c6b565940bdcad889&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1767447732985-694e12cb-aacb-47b6-9886-dd15617ab1ee.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=4407041111201658999&skey=@crypt_c5903577_3de2ba57d9640c4c6b565940bdcad889&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1767447739065-e1f54fbe-3ea5-40f4-9ac1-f18d729e0e8d.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=5261064777157213169&skey=@crypt_c5903577_3de2ba57d9640c4c6b565940bdcad889&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1767447744867-b7b0966f-ed5c-4e25-8dc4-d08c102b60f5.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

绍兴市出租车型号统一且涂装样式较有特色（类似省会杭州），部分车顶灯有超大电子显示屏，较好辨认。

##### 5.湖州市

- 绿银   大众桑塔纳居多

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=2008723359977371269&skey=@crypt_c5903577_d444a6425a1580bddfadc202b63c5877&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1775280177069-25e5b955-1a9e-4b59-bb79-77840bbc4ac0.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=167151802708913202&skey=@crypt_c5903577_d444a6425a1580bddfadc202b63c5877&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1775280195616-e2ac26bc-cb3f-46a6-b3ee-37748f76cb65.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_29%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

绿银出租车为波浪形分色，且车侧印字为蓝色。

- 蓝银   吉利帝豪ev450（新能源车）

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=8063553910640195956&skey=@crypt_c5903577_d444a6425a1580bddfadc202b63c5877&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1775280206286-e1802542-4815-4879-bb9e-f9712fb09996.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_26%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

蓝银出租车顶灯有较大电子显示屏，车侧图案为白色。

- 蓝白   比亚迪E5、E6（新能源车）

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=8578846221662587348&skey=@crypt_c5903577_d444a6425a1580bddfadc202b63c5877&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1775280212435-f605cff3-142a-45ea-8c4b-74ab315ff75e.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=1928559505642907124&skey=@crypt_c5903577_d444a6425a1580bddfadc202b63c5877&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1775280219782-fa1fcb05-3e88-4067-9f72-c4e330445e90.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

蓝白出租车也都为波浪形分色，其中比亚迪E5顶灯样式与宁波相同，E6则为蓝-白-蓝相间涂装。

#### 福建省

##### 1.福州市

- 车型种类丰富，其中大众捷达/桑塔纳（图一图五图六）居多

福州市出租车配色种类较多，其中绿银数量最多。顶灯右侧通常会有一块蓝色部分，一些车在引擎盖上印有大号“TAXI”字样，较好辨认。

##### 2.莆田市

- 主要为大众桑塔纳（图一至三、图五）和标致301（图六）。新能源车为云度π3（图七）和启辰D60ev两款车型

莆田市出租车部分车型选取的较有特色，但在配色涂饰等方面略显平庸，且全市出租车在街景中的能见度不高，最好在出租车的基础上寻找题目中更多信息来定位莆田市。

##### 3.泉州市

- 主要为大众桑塔纳（图一图六）和多品牌绿牌新能源车（如图二欧拉 图四荣威 图五比亚迪等）

泉州市出租车配色较为统一，且分色样式略有特色，易于辨认。

厦门市出租车虽然型号配色种类丰富，但涂装较有特色，引擎盖上印的"TAXI"是其醒目特征，较好辨认。

##### 5.漳州市

- 主要为大众捷达/桑塔纳（图一）、起亚锐欧（图二）和赛拉图（图三图四）

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=3846230111087876023&skey=@crypt_c5903577_d444a6425a1580bddfadc202b63c5877&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1775281568201-637fe69a-06ae-4ca8-8faf-5fb77c116ff6.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_31%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

漳州市出租车型号较为统一，车侧印字多为弧形，花状图案亦是其特点。

#### 广东省

##### 1.广州市

- 早期现代悦动（图一）和索纳塔（图七）居多；新的均为绿牌新能源车，主要为广汽埃安S（图六图十一）、GE3（图九）和北汽绅宝D50（图五），也有不少其他品牌

广州市出租车虽然型号配色较多不易记忆，但其鱼鳍状的顶灯很有特色，可由它从而定位广州市。

##### 2.深圳市

- 早期主要为丰田花冠（图一）、大众朗逸（图二）及桑塔纳（图三），新出租车为新旧两款比亚迪E6

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738332322910-3e114bc3-9c4a-4574-8aab-91abb002cbd1.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738332466533-d2ccbbc4-a18c-4d9c-be3e-955b56e0f00b.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738332496401-08aec8ab-f62c-4920-8fd4-abbf9fc6bc0d.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738332549843-ef27be32-a550-4de1-b090-1d92c9007ec1.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_31%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738332564580-fbfe7e90-ca31-4783-b8ff-7cf1f8e946e8.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_14%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738332756067-65f0b8d8-9682-4334-8c34-d7e6cedc4387.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738332768778-ced9fbb2-353e-4b61-ac3d-604b63b248a6.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

深圳市出租车车型配色较为统一，早期配色为绿银和红银（均弧形分色），且二者车型相同。后期统一为新旧两款蓝白E6（并存），顶灯均有深圳字样，车侧印着其所属公司名称以及黄色的叫车电话，易于辨认。

太原、安阳、武汉（武汉能见度较低）等地均有比亚迪E6车型，但它们顶灯、车侧涂饰以及分色样式都不大一样

##### 3.珠海市

- 早期基本上是大众老捷达（图一）和比亚迪E6（图二）。新街景中主要为大众捷达（图三）、日产轩逸（图四）以及多品牌绿牌新能源车（如图五 比亚迪E5、图六吉利帝豪ev450等）

![837acf6de5839c68bde01f4293fc52f4.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756632514857-1b150fb1-edf0-4f05-89ac-9de08ddcc366.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_31%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![6823c1bc10ee689e2d3e029ffb0e4076.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756632526565-2027eed4-59c0-4282-bc87-7edf1ab24847.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_33%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

珠海市出租车配色较为统一，但车型种类丰富。顶灯大多为黄色且有着“珠海”字样，车侧也有印着白色的公司名称和编号，较好辨认。

##### 4.汕头市

- 主要为吉利帝豪 ev450（图一图二）和现代伊兰特（图三至五）

汕头市出租车配色种类丰富，部分车在车侧或顶灯印有”汕头”“汕运”字样，易于定位。

##### 5.佛山市

- 主要为大众桑塔纳（图一），有部分比亚迪E6（图二）、丰田卡罗拉等车型

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=5499254945121695512&skey=@crypt_c5903577_d444a6425a1580bddfadc202b63c5877&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1775282194256-224c646f-c220-4c24-a3ac-9cbbe9bb0c1e.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_28%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![_cgi-bin_mmwebwx-bin_webwxgetmsgimg__&MsgID=5899788616728981906&skey=@crypt_c5903577_d444a6425a1580bddfadc202b63c5877&mmweb_appid=wx_webfilehelper.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2026/jpeg/42695345/1775282204509-06ccbabe-c80b-407b-980f-cbb023361306.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_39%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

佛山市出租车配色统一为红银，车侧的各式贴纸图案是其醒目特征，易于辨认。

#### 海南省

##### 1.海口市

- 基本上是海马海福星（图一）、M8（图二）和福美来M5（图三图四）。新的为荣威Ei5（图六）（旧涂装仍使用）

![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/jpeg/35193536/1707735976711-5b7563eb-e2c6-4f95-80c0-6a31e602489a.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_24%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/jpeg/35193536/1707735977246-4f8ce0f1-dcea-4939-b3b2-6abc298723ae.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_25%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/42695345/1738317412622-418da129-9138-485d-be1d-f9b4be8fc62a.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_26%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![f77e3fca00a393dd478c8c2c4d806288.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756083021992-be430e8d-a697-4e30-bdc0-321b5a0065bb.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_28%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![fb69782ffd62cb0b3aed7db9db834547.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1756083065987-87b8810f-ac06-4ba7-939f-2763d6778653.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_34%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

海口市出租车配色种类较多，但车型品牌较统一，且车前方均有绿色牌子，较好辨认。

##### 2.三亚市

- 以大众捷达、起亚赛拉图和现代伊兰特为主

![bb36bf2f7f9ae5a7f57efdfe5fff86e.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754117007286-7e1bf0dc-da8f-422e-b8f2-22e6aca9dd35.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![95315c0b5dc4aca2651bca53290b9fa.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754117041713-60c179b8-e071-4788-abad-b593202f8b93.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![420821d734d97977d73e13070f9d79a.jpg](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/jpeg/42695345/1754117187268-911a4a10-2ce8-4c74-be04-1fcf2535fe7b.jpeg?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

三亚市出租车配色种类较多，其中全橙能见度最高。车前后均有和海口一样的绿色牌子，易于辨认。
